<1308218750864064584> [05:53 PM 11/18/24] Message Sent: # S K I N S
<1308218800054734920> [05:54 PM 11/18/24] Message Sent: Skins (stylized as SKINS) 

The third studio album by American rapper Jahseh Onfroy, or “XXXTENTACION”

 It was released on December 7, 2018 through Bad Vibes Forever and Empire Distribution. It is one of the projects, that Onfroy worked on before his death in summer of 2018, and was released posthumously. The album features guest appearances from Travis Barker of Blink-182 and Kanye West. The album's theme sees XXXTentacion discuss heartbreak and mental turmoil. Genres on the album draw influence from lo-fi, nu metal, screamo, emo, punk rock, ambient, trap and acoustic. 

Skins was leaked to the internet three days before its official release date.

I do not care who you are whether you are a mod or not. Do not make these types of jokes in these servers and if you’re a good enough person I expect you to not make them at all. You’re a horrible person if you say you hope someone gets raped.  If you even find rape funny then just leave the server on your own.

7. Do not post your links in any other chat besides the self promo chat. This means any SoundCloud rappers, guns.lol accounts, server links, TikTok links. (if the link isn’t your video then do with it while you will.)

8. Have fun, but not to much. We are not strict at all but if you get outta line we will take action depending on what you did. 

Thank you, and enjoy your time in skins :D
